# Entramos al contenedor
docker exec -it psql_docker psql -U postgres

# Creamos usuario y base de datos
create user psql_user superuser password 'datahub';
create database data_lake;
exit;

# Accedemos a la base de datos con nuestro usuario
docker exec -it psql_docker psql -d data_lake -U psql_user

# Creamos los esquemas
create schema etl_tool;
create schema northwind;
create schema northwind_dv;
create schema northwind_dm;


# Creamos las tablas e insertamos los datos


set search_path to northwind;

CREATE TABLE CATEGORIES (	
    CATEGORY_ID INT NOT NULL, 
	CATEGORY_NAME VARCHAR(15) NOT NULL, 
	DESCRIPTION VARCHAR(2000), 
	PICTURE VARCHAR(255), 
	PRIMARY KEY (CATEGORY_ID)
);

CREATE TABLE CUSTOMERS (
    CUSTOMER_ID INT NOT NULL,
    CUSTOMER_CODE VARCHAR(5) NOT NULL,
    COMPANY_NAME VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL,
    CONTACT_NAME VARCHAR(30),
    CONTACT_TITLE VARCHAR(30),
    ADDRESS VARCHAR(60),
    CITY VARCHAR(15),
    REGION VARCHAR(15),
    POSTAL_CODE VARCHAR(10),
    COUNTRY VARCHAR(15),
    PHONE VARCHAR(24),
    FAX VARCHAR(24),
    PRIMARY KEY (CUSTOMER_ID)
);

CREATE TABLE EMPLOYEES (
	EMPLOYEE_ID int NOT NULL,
	LASTNAME varchar(20) NOT NULL,
	FIRSTNAME varchar(10) NOT NULL,
	TITLE varchar(30),
	TITLE_OF_COURTESY varchar(25),
	BIRTHDATE date,
	HIREDATE date,
	ADDRESS varchar(60),
	CITY varchar(15),
	REGION varchar(15),
	POSTAL_CODE varchar(10),
	COUNTRY varchar(15),
	HOME_PHONE varchar(24),
	EXTENSION varchar(4),
	PHOTO varchar(255),
	NOTES varchar(2000),
	REPORTS_TO int,
	PRIMARY KEY (EMPLOYEE_ID)
);

CREATE TABLE ORDER_DETAILS
( 
	ORDER_ID INT NOT NULL,
	PRODUCT_ID INT NOT NULL,
	UNIT_PRICE DECIMAL(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00' NOT NULL,
	QUANTITY INT DEFAULT '1' NOT NULL,
	DISCOUNT DECIMAL(4,2) DEFAULT '0.00' NOT NULL,
	CONSTRAINT CK_ORDER_DETAILS_UNIT_PRICE CHECK (Unit_Price>=0),
	CONSTRAINT CK_ORDER_DETAILS_QUANTITY CHECK (Quantity>0),
	CONSTRAINT CK_ORDER_DETAILS_DISCOUNT CHECK (Discount between 0 and 1),
	PRIMARY KEY (ORDER_ID, PRODUCT_ID));

CREATE TABLE ORDERS (
  ORDER_ID INT NOT NULL,
  CUSTOMER_ID INT NOT NULL,
  EMPLOYEE_ID INT NOT NULL,
  ORDER_DATE DATE NOT NULL,
  REQUIRED_DATE DATE,
  SHIPPED_DATE DATE,
  SHIP_VIA INT,
  FREIGHT decimal(10,2) DEFAULT 0,
  SHIP_NAME VARCHAR(40),
  SHIP_ADDRESS VARCHAR(60),
  SHIP_CITY VARCHAR(15),
  SHIP_REGION VARCHAR(15),
  SHIP_POSTAL_CODE VARCHAR(10),
  SHIP_COUNTRY VARCHAR(15),
  PRIMARY KEY (ORDER_ID)
);

CREATE TABLE PRODUCTS
( PRODUCT_ID INT NOT NULL,
PRODUCT_NAME VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL,
SUPPLIER_ID INT NOT NULL,
CATEGORY_ID INT NOT NULL,
QUANTITY_PER_UNIT VARCHAR(20),
UNIT_PRICE DECIMAL(10,2) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
UNITS_IN_STOCK INT DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
UNITS_ON_ORDER INT DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
REORDER_LEVEL INT DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
DISCONTINUED CHAR(1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
CONSTRAINT CK_PRODUCTS_UNIT_PRICE CHECK (Unit_Price>=0),
CONSTRAINT CK_PRODUCTS_UNITS_IN_STOCK CHECK (Units_In_Stock>=0),
CONSTRAINT CK_PRODUCTS_UNITS_ON_ORDER CHECK (Units_On_Order>=0),
CONSTRAINT CK_PRODUCTS_REORDER_LEVEL CHECK (Reorder_Level>=0),
CONSTRAINT CK_PRODUCTS_DISCONTINUED CHECK (Discontinued in ('Y','N')),
CONSTRAINT PK_PRODUCTS PRIMARY KEY (PRODUCT_ID));

# HUBS


create table category_hub as 
	select 
		md5(cast(category_id as varchar)) category_hub_hashkey,
		category_id,
		now() load_date,
		'northwind' record_source
	from northwind.categories;


create table customer_hub as 
	select 
		md5(cast(customer_id as varchar)) customer_hub_hashkey,
		customer_id,
		now() load_date,
		'northwind' record_source
	from northwind.customers;


create table employee_hub as 
	select 
		md5(cast(employee_id as varchar)) employee_hub_hashkey,
		employee_id,
		now() load_date,
		'northwind' record_source
	from northwind.employees;


create table order_hub as 
	select 
		md5(cast(order_id as varchar)) order_hub_hashkey,
		order_id,
		now() load_date,
		'northwind' record_source
	from northwind.orders;


create table product_hub as 
	select 
		md5(cast(product_id as varchar)) product_hub_hashkey,
		product_id,
		now() load_date,
		'northwind' record_source
	from northwind.products;


create table shipper_hub as 
	select 
		md5(cast(shipper_id as varchar)) shipper_hub_hashkey,
		shipper_id,
		now() load_date,
		'northwind' record_source
	from northwind.shippers;


create table supplier_hub as 
	select 
		md5(cast(supplier_id as varchar)) supplier_hub_hashkey,
		supplier_id,
		now() load_date,
		'northwind' record_source
	from northwind.suppliers;


# LINKS


create table northwind_dv.order_detail_link as 
	select 
		md5(
			cast(order_id as varchar) || cast(product_id as varchar)) order_detail_link_hashkey,
		now() load_date,
		'northwind' record_source,
		md5(cast(order_id as varchar)) order_hub_hashkey,
		md5(cast(product_id as varchar)) product_hub_hashkey
	from northwind.order_details;


create table northwind_dv.order_link as 
	select 
		md5(
			cast(order_id as varchar) || cast(customer_id as varchar) || 
			cast(employee_id as varchar) || cast(ship_via as varchar)) order_link_hashkey,
		now() load_date,
		'northwind' record_source,
		md5(cast(order_id as varchar)) order_hub_hashkey,
		md5(cast(customer_id as varchar)) customer_hub_hashkey,
		md5(cast(employee_id as varchar)) employee_hub_hashkey,
		md5(cast(ship_via as varchar)) shipper_hub_hashkey
	from northwind.orders;


create table northwind_dv.product_category_link as 
	select 
		md5(
			cast(product_id as varchar) || cast(category_id as varchar)) product_category_link_hashkey,
		now() load_date,
		'northwind' record_source,
		md5(cast(product_id as varchar)) product_hub_hashkey,
		md5(cast(category_id as varchar)) category_hub_hashkey
	from northwind.products;


create table northwind_dv.product_supplier_link as 
	select 
		md5(
			cast(product_id as varchar) || cast(supplier_id as varchar)) product_supplier_link_hashkey,
		now() load_date,
		'northwind' record_source,
		md5(cast(product_id as varchar)) product_hub_hashkey,
		md5(cast(supplier_id as varchar)) supplier_hub_hashkey
	from northwind.products;



# SATS


create table northwind_dv.category_sat as
	select 
		md5(cast(category_id as varchar)) category_hub_hashkey,
		now() load_date,
		'northwind' record_source,
		category_name,
		description
	from northwind.categories;


create table northwind_dv.customer_sat as
	select 
		md5(cast(customer_id as varchar)) customer_hub_hashkey,
		now() load_date,
		'northwind' record_source,
		customer_code,
		company_name,
		contact_name,
		contact_title,
		address,
		city,
		region,
		postal_code,
		country,
		phone,
		fax
	from northwind.customers;


create table northwind_dv.employee_sat as
	select 
		md5(cast(employee_id as varchar)) employee_hub_hashkey,
		now() load_date,
		'northwind' record_source,
		lastname,
		firstname,
		title,
		title_of_courtesy,
		birthdate,
		hiredate,
		address,
		city,
		region,
		postal_code,
		country
	from northwind.employees;


create table northwind_dv.order_detail_sat as
	select 
		md5(
			cast(order_id as varchar) || cast(product_id as varchar)) order_detail_link_hashkey,
		now() load_date,
		'northwind' record_source,
		unit_price,
		quantity,
		discount
	from northwind.order_details;


create table northwind_dv.order_sat as
	select 
		md5(
			cast(order_id as varchar) || cast(customer_id as varchar) || 
			cast(employee_id as varchar) || cast(ship_via as varchar)) order_link_hashkey,
		now() load_date,
		'northwind' record_source,
		order_date,
		required_date,
		shipped_date,
		freight,
		ship_name,
		ship_address,
		ship_city,
		ship_region,
		ship_postal_code,
		ship_country
	from northwind.orders;


create table northwind_dv.product_sat as
	select 
		md5(cast(product_id as varchar)) product_hub_hashkey,
		now() load_date,
		'northwind' record_source,
		product_name,
		quantity_per_unit,
		unit_price,
		units_in_stock,
		units_on_order,
		reorder_level,
		discontinued
	from northwind.products;


create table northwind_dv.shipper_sat as
	select 
		md5(cast(shipper_id as varchar)) shipper_hub_hashkey,
		now() load_date,
		'northwind' record_source,
		company_name,
		phone
	from northwind.shippers;


create table northwind_dv.supplier_sat as
	select 
		md5(cast(supplier_id as varchar)) supplier_hub_hashkey,
		now() load_date,
		'northwind' record_source,
		company_name,
		contact_name,
		contact_title,
		address,
		city,
		region,
		postal_code,
		country
	from northwind.suppliers;

CREATE TABLE DIM_DIA 
   (	IDDIA INT NOT NULL , 
	IDMES INT NOT NULL , 
	IDTRIMESTRE INT NOT NULL , 
	IDSEMESTRE INT NOT NULL , 
	IDANO INT NOT NULL , 
	DIA DATE NOT NULL , 
	DIAANO INT NOT NULL , 
	DIAMES INT NOT NULL , 
	NUMDIASEM INT NOT NULL , 
	DIASEMABR VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL , 
	DIASEM VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL , 
	SEMANO INT NOT NULL , 
	NOMMES VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL , 
	NUMMES INT NOT NULL , 
	TRIMESTRE INT NOT NULL , 
	SEMESTRE INT NOT NULL , 
	ANO INT NOT NULL , 
	QUINCENA INT NOT NULL , 
	ESTACION VARCHAR(30), 
	 CONSTRAINT XPKDIA PRIMARY KEY (IDDIA));

CREATE TABLE DIM_MES 
   (	IDMES INT NOT NULL , 
	IDTRIMESTRE INT NOT NULL , 
	IDSEMESTRE INT NOT NULL , 
	IDANO INT NOT NULL , 
	NOMMES VARCHAR NOT NULL , 
	NUMMES INT NOT NULL , 
	TRIMESTRE INT NOT NULL , 
	SEMESTRE INT NOT NULL , 
	ANO INT NOT NULL , 
	DIA DATE, 
	DATACARGA DATE NOT NULL , 
	 CONSTRAINT XPKMES PRIMARY KEY (IDMES));

   (	ID_PEDIDO INT NOT NULL , 
	ID_PRODUCTO INT NOT NULL ,

	COD_PEDIDO INT, 
	FECHA_CARGA DATE, 
	ID_EMPLEADO INT NOT NULL , 
	 CONSTRAINT HE_PEDIDOS_PK PRIMARY KEY (ID_PEDIDO));
